                     <img src="/UserFiles/Servers/Server_6/Image/Theme/RotatingBannerImages/UrbanGreen_Banner_Summer_940x300.jpg" title="#htmlcaption1"/>
                    </a>
                    <a href="http://www.cityoftacoma.org/cms/one.aspx?portalId=169&amp;pageId=28444">
                     <img src="/UserFiles/Servers/Server_6/Image/Theme/RotatingBannerImages/Fireworks_Banner-2018_940x300.jpg" title="#htmlcaption2"/>
                    </a>
                    <a href="http://www.cityoftacoma.org/cms/One.aspx?portalId=169&amp;pageId=140797 ">
                     <img src="/UserFiles/Servers/Server_6/Image/Theme/RotatingBannerImages/Sustainability Small Grant Rotating Banner_940x300.jpg" title="#htmlcaption3"/>
                    </a>
                    <a href="http://tacomapermits.org/">
                     <img src="/UserFiles/Servers/Server_6/Image/Theme/RotatingBannerImages/TacPerm_940x300-min.jpg" title="#htmlcaption4"/>
                    </a>
                   </div>
                   <div class="nivo-html-caption" id="htmlcaption1">
                    <a href="http://www.cityoftacoma.org/UrbanGreen ">
                     The summer edition of Urban Green is playing now online and on TV Tacoma!
                    </a>
                   </div>
                   <div class="nivo-html-caption" id="htmlcaption2">
                    <a href="http://www.cityoftacoma.org/cms/one.aspx?portalId=169&amp;pageId=28444">
                     Personal fireworks use is banned in the City of Tacoma. Violators are subject to a $257 fine and the confiscation of their fireworks.
                    </a>
                   </div>
                   <div class="nivo-html-caption" id="htmlcaption3">
                    <a href="http://www.cityoftacoma.org/cms/One.aspx?portalId=169&amp;pageId=140797 ">
                     Apply for a Sustainability Small Grant today! Applications due June 30, 2018.
                    </a>
                   </div>
                   <div class="nivo-html-caption" id="htmlcaption4">
                    <a href="http://tacomapermits.org/">
                     Changes have been to the Single-Family Permitting Process as of June 1. For more on the update, visit tacomapermits.org.
                    </a>
                   </div>

    <script type="text/javascript">
     $(window).load(function() {
   var watermark = 'Search...';
   //init, set watermark text and class
   $('input.gsc-input').val(watermark).addClass('watermark');
   //if blur and no value inside, set watermark text and class again.
   $('input.gsc-input').blur(function(){
       if ($(this).val().length == 0){
         $(this).val(watermark).addClass('watermark');
     }
   });
   //if focus and text is watermrk, set it to empty and remove the watermark class
   $('input.gsc-input').focus(function(){
       if ($(this).val() == watermark){
         $(this).val('').removeClass('watermark');
     }
   });
 });
    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
     function homeAccordian() {                  $('.row').find('.col').find('.ptl_portlet_vertical:eq(0)').click(function(){
                     if ($(window).width() <= 651) {   
                     if ($(this).next().css("display") == "none") {        
                     $('.ptl_portlet_vertical').not(this).next().slideUp();
                     $(this).next().slideDown();
                     }
                     else {
                     $(this).next().slideUp();
                     }
                     } 
                     })
                     }
                     $(document).ready(homeAccordian);
                     $(window).resize(function(){
                     if ($(window).width() > 950) {   
                     $('.row .col .ptl_portlet_vertical').show();
                     }
                     })
    </script>
